<pr_description>
bug(cli): sandbox create with duplicate name returns raw database error instead of user-friendly message
## agent diagnostic

- loaded `openshell-cli` skill — checked `sandbox create --help` for `--force`/`--replace`/`--overwrite` flags; none exist
- loaded `debug-openshell-cluster` skill — cluster is healthy (`openshell status` and `openshell doctor check` both pass)
- confirmed workaround: `sandbox delete <name>` then `sandbox create --name <name>` works, but the error message gives no hint to do this
- agent cannot resolve: the error originates in the grpc server layer — sqlite unique constraint error (code 2067) is surfaced as a raw `internal` grpc status instead of being caught and mapped to `alreadyexists` with a human-readable message. this requires a server-side code change in the persist layer or grpc handler.

## description

**actual behavior:** creating a sandbox with a name that already exists returns a raw internal error exposing sqlite internals and grpc metadata:

```
error: × status: Internal, message: "persist sandbox failed: execution error:
  database error: error returned from database: (code: 2067) UNIQUE
  constraint failed: objects.object_type, objects.name", details: [],
  metadata: MetadataMap { headers: {"content-type": "application/grpc",
  "date": "Mon, 30 Mar 2026 23:51:20 GMT"} }
```

**expected behavior:** a clear, actionable error like:

```
error: sandbox 'dupe-test' already exists

hint: delete it first with: openshell sandbox delete dupe-test
      or use a different name
```

## reproduction steps

1. `openshell sandbox create --name dupe-test --no-tty -- sleep 120 &`
2. wait for sandbox to reach `ready` phase (`openshell sandbox list`)
3. `openshell sandbox create --name dupe-test --no-tty -- echo "second"`
4. observe raw database error instead of "already exists" message

## environment

- os: macos 26.3.1 (darwin, apple silicon)
- docker: docker desktop 29.2.1
- openshell: v0.0.6

## logs

```
$ openshell sandbox create --name dupe-test --no-tty -- echo "second"

  │ metadata: MetadataMap { headers: {"content-type": "application/grpc",
  │ "date": "Mon, 30 Mar 2026 23:51:20 GMT"} }
```

    22	    pub name: String,

    42	/// Persistence store implementations.
    43	#[derive(Debug, Clone)]
    44	pub enum Store {
    45	    Postgres(PostgresStore),
    46	    Sqlite(SqliteStore),
    47	}
    48

    51	    fn object_type() -> &'static str;
    52	}

    57	}

    62	}

    64	/// Generate a random 6-character lowercase alphabetic name.
    65	pub fn generate_name() -> String {
    66	    let mut rng = rand::rng();
    67	    (0..6)
    68	        .map(|_| rng.random_range(b'a'..=b'z') as char)
    69	        .collect()
    70	}
    71	
    72	impl Store {
    73	    /// Connect to a persistence store based on the database URL.
    74	    pub async fn connect(url: &str) -> Result<Self> {
    75	        if url.starts_with("postgres://") || url.starts_with("postgresql://") {
    76	            let store = PostgresStore::connect(url).await?;
    77	            store.migrate().await?;
    78	            Ok(Self::Postgres(store))
    79	        } else if url.starts_with("sqlite:") {
    80	            let store = SqliteStore::connect(url).await?;
    81	            store.migrate().await?;
    82	            Ok(Self::Sqlite(store))
    83	        } else {
    84	            Err(Error::config(format!(
    85	                "unsupported database URL scheme: {url}"
    86	            )))
    87	        }
    88	    }
    89	
    90	    /// Insert or update an object.
    91	    pub async fn put(&self, object_type: &str, id: &str, name: &str, payload: &[u8]) -> Result<()> {
    92	        match self {
    93	            Self::Postgres(store) => store.put(object_type, id, name, payload).await,
    94	            Self::Sqlite(store) => store.put(object_type, id, name, payload).await,
    95	        }
    96	    }

    19	    pub async fn connect(url: &str) -> Result<Self> {
    20	        let max_connections = if url.contains(":memory:") || url.contains("mode=memory") {
    21	            1
    22	        } else {
    23	            5
    24	        };
    25	
    26	        let options = SqliteConnectOptions::from_str(url)
    27	            .map_err(|e| map_db_error(&e))?
    28	            .create_if_missing(true);
    29	
    30	        let pool = SqlitePoolOptions::new()
    31	            .max_connections(max_connections)
    32	            .min_connections(max_connections)
    33	            .connect_with(options)
    34	            .await
    35	            .map_err(|e| map_db_error(&e))?;
    36	
    37	        Ok(Self { pool })
    38	    }

    56	        sqlx::query(

    60	ON CONFLICT ("id") DO UPDATE SET
    61	    "payload" = excluded."payload",
    62	    "updated_at_ms" = excluded."updated_at_ms"
    63	WHERE "objects"."object_type" = excluded."object_type"
    64	"#,
    65	        )
    66	        .bind(object_type)
    67	        .bind(id)
    68	        .bind(name)
    69	        .bind(payload)
    70	        .bind(now_ms)
    71	        .execute(&self.pool)
    72	        .await
    73	        .map_err(|e| map_db_error(&e))?;

   258	    /// Insert or update a protobuf message using its inferred object type, id, and name.
   259	    pub async fn put_message<T: Message + ObjectType + ObjectId + ObjectName>(
   260	        &self,
   261	        message: &T,
   262	    ) -> Result<()> {
   263	        self.put(
   264	            T::object_type(),
   265	            message.object_id(),
   266	            message.object_name(),
   267	            &message.encode_to_vec(),
   268	        )
   269	        .await
   270	    }

   272	    /// Fetch and decode a protobuf message by id.
   273	    pub async fn get_message<T: Message + Default + ObjectType>(
   274	        &self,
   275	        id: &str,
   276	    ) -> Result<Option<T>> {
   277	        let record = self.get(T::object_type(), id).await?;
   278	        let Some(record) = record else {
   279	            return Ok(None);
   280	        };
   281	
   282	        T::decode(record.payload.as_slice())
   283	            .map(Some)
   284	            .map_err(|e| Error::execution(format!("protobuf decode error: {e}")))
   285	    }
   286	
   287	    /// Fetch and decode a protobuf message by name.
   288	    pub async fn get_message_by_name<T: Message + Default + ObjectType>(
   289	        &self,
   290	        name: &str,
   291	    ) -> Result<Option<T>> {
   292	        let record = self.get_by_name(T::object_type(), name).await?;
   293	        let Some(record) = record else {
   294	            return Ok(None);
   295	        };
   296	
   297	        T::decode(record.payload.as_slice())
   298	            .map(Some)
   299	            .map_err(|e| Error::execution(format!("protobuf decode error: {e}")))
   300	    }

   408	fn current_time_ms() -> Result<i64> {
   409	    let now = SystemTime::now()
   410	        .duration_since(UNIX_EPOCH)
   411	        .map_err(|e| Error::execution(format!("time error: {e}")))?;
   412	    i64::try_from(now.as_millis())
   413	        .map_err(|e| Error::execution(format!("time conversion error: {e}")))
   414	}

   417	    Error::execution(format!("database error: {error}"))
   418	}

   421	    Error::execution(format!("migration error: {error}"))

     4	//! Common error types for OpenShell.
     5	
     6	use miette::Diagnostic;
     7	use thiserror::Error;
     8	
     9	/// Result type alias using OpenShell's error type.
    10	pub type Result<T> = std::result::Result<T, Error>;
    11	
    12	/// OpenShell error type.
    13	#[derive(Debug, Error, Diagnostic)]
    14	pub enum Error {
    15	    /// Configuration error.
    16	    #[error("configuration error: {message}")]
    17	    #[diagnostic(code(openshell::config))]
    18	    Config {
    19	        /// Error message.
    20	        message: String,
    21	    },
    22	
    23	    /// I/O error.
    24	    #[error("I/O error: {source}")]
    25	    #[diagnostic(code(openshell::io))]
    26	    Io {
    27	        /// Underlying I/O error.
    28	        #[from]
    29	        source: std::io::Error,
    30	    },
    31	
    32	    /// TLS error.
    33	    #[error("TLS error: {message}")]
    34	    #[diagnostic(code(openshell::tls))]
    35	    Tls {
    36	        /// Error message.
    37	        message: String,
    38	    },
    39	
    40	    /// gRPC transport error.
    41	    #[error("transport error: {message}")]
    42	    #[diagnostic(code(openshell::transport))]
    43	    Transport {
    44	        /// Error message.
    45	        message: String,
    46	    },
    47	
    48	    /// Execution error.
    49	    #[error("execution error: {message}")]
    50	    #[diagnostic(code(openshell::execution))]
    51	    Execution {
    52	        /// Error message.
    53	        message: String,
    54	    },
    55	
    56	    /// Process error.
    57	    #[error("process error: {message}")]
    58	    #[diagnostic(code(openshell::process))]
    59	    Process {
    60	        /// Error message.
    61	        message: String,
    62	    },
    63	
    64	    /// Timeout error.
    65	    #[error("operation timed out")]
    66	    #[diagnostic(code(openshell::timeout))]
    67	    Timeout,
    68	}
    69

    71	    /// Create a configuration error.
    72	    pub fn config(message: impl Into<String>) -> Self {
    73	        Self::Config {
    74	            message: message.into(),
    75	        }
    76	    }
    77	
    78	    /// Create a TLS error.

    82	        }
    83	    }

    89	        }
    90	    }

    96	        }

   143	/// Clamp a client-provided page `limit`.
   144	///
   145	/// Returns `default` when `raw` is 0 (the protobuf zero-value convention),
   146	/// otherwise returns the smaller of `raw` and `max`.
   147	pub fn clamp_limit(raw: u32, default: u32, max: u32) -> u32 {
   148	    if raw == 0 { default } else { raw.min(max) }
   149	}

   167	impl OpenShell for OpenShellService {
   168	    async fn health(
   169	        &self,
   170	        _request: Request<HealthRequest>,
   171	    ) -> Result<Response<HealthResponse>, Status> {
   172	        Ok(Response::new(HealthResponse {
   173	            status: ServiceStatus::Healthy.into(),
   174	            version: openshell_core::VERSION.to_string(),
   175	        }))
   176	    }
   177	
   178	    async fn create_sandbox(
   179	        &self,
   180	        request: Request<CreateSandboxRequest>,
   181	    ) -> Result<Response<SandboxResponse>, Status> {
   182	        let request = request.into_inner();
   183	        let spec = request
   184	            .spec
   185	            .ok_or_else(|| Status::invalid_argument("spec is required"))?;
   186	
   187	        // Validate field sizes before any I/O (fail fast on oversized payloads).
   188	        validate_sandbox_spec(&request.name, &spec)?;
   189	
   190	        // Validate provider names exist (fail fast). Credentials are fetched at
   191	        // runtime by the sandbox supervisor via GetSandboxProviderEnvironment.
   192	        for name in &spec.providers {
   193	            self.state
   194	                .store
   195	                .get_message_by_name::<Provider>(name)
   196	                .await
   197	                .map_err(|e| Status::internal(format!("fetch provider failed: {e}")))?
   198	                .ok_or_else(|| {
   199	                    Status::failed_precondition(format!("provider '{name}' not found"))
   200	                })?;
   201	        }
   202	
   203	        // Ensure the template always carries the resolved image so clients
   204	        // (CLI, TUI, etc.) can read the actual image from the stored sandbox.
   205	        let mut spec = spec;
   206	        let template = spec.template.get_or_insert_with(SandboxTemplate::default);
   207	        if template.image.is_empty() {
   208	            template.image = self.state.sandbox_client.default_image().to_string();
   209	        }
   210	
   211	        if spec.gpu {
   212	            self.state
   213	                .sandbox_client
   214	                .validate_gpu_support()
   215	                .await
   216	                .map_err(|status| {
   217	                    warn!(error = %status, "Rejecting GPU sandbox request");
   218	                    status
   219	                })?;
   220	        }
   221	
   222	        // Ensure process identity defaults to "sandbox" when missing or
   223	        // empty, then validate policy safety before persisting.
   224	        if let Some(ref mut policy) = spec.policy {
   225	            openshell_policy::ensure_sandbox_process_identity(policy);
   226	            validate_policy_safety(policy)?;
   227	        }
   228	
   229	        let id = uuid::Uuid::new_v4().to_string();
   230	        let name = if request.name.is_empty() {
   231	            petname::petname(2, "-").unwrap_or_else(generate_name)
   232	        } else {
   233	            request.name.clone()
   234	        };
   235	        let namespace = self.state.config.sandbox_namespace.clone();
   236	
   237	        let sandbox = Sandbox {
   238	            id: id.clone(),
   239	            name: name.clone(),
   240	            namespace,
   241	            spec: Some(spec),
   242	            status: None,
   243	            phase: SandboxPhase::Provisioning as i32,
   244	            ..Default::default()
   245	        };
   246	
   247	        // Persist to the store FIRST so the sandbox watcher always finds
   248	        // the record with `spec` populated.  If we created the k8s
   249	        // resource first, the watcher could race us and write a fallback
   250	        // record with `spec: None`, causing the supervisor to fail with
   251	        // "sandbox has no spec".
   252	        self.state.sandbox_index.update_from_sandbox(&sandbox);
   253	
   254	        self.state
   255	            .store
   256	            .put_message(&sandbox)
   257	            .await
   258	            .map_err(|e| Status::internal(format!("persist sandbox failed: {e}")))?;
   259	
   260	        // Now create the Kubernetes resource.  If this fails, clean up
   261	        // the store entry to avoid orphans.
   262	        match self.state.sandbox_client.create(&sandbox).await {
   263	            Ok(_) => {}
   264	            Err(kube::Error::Api(err)) if err.code == 409 => {
   265	                // Clean up the store entry we just wrote.
   266	                let _ = self.state.store.delete("sandbox", &id).await;
   267	                self.state.sandbox_index.remove_sandbox(&id);
   268	                warn!(
   269	                    sandbox_id = %id,
   270	                    sandbox_name = %name,
   271	                    "Sandbox already exists in Kubernetes"
   272	                );
   273	                return Err(Status::already_exists("sandbox already exists"));
   274	            }
   275	            Err(err) => {
   276	                // Clean up the store entry we just wrote.
   277	                let _ = self.state.store.delete("sandbox", &id).await;
   278	                self.state.sandbox_index.remove_sandbox(&id);
   279	                warn!(
   280	                    sandbox_id = %id,
   281	                    sandbox_name = %name,
   282	                    error = %err,
   283	                    "CreateSandbox request failed"
   284	                );
   285	                return Err(Status::internal(format!(
   286	                    "create sandbox in kubernetes failed: {err}"
   287	                )));
   288	            }
   289	        }
   290	
   291	        self.state.sandbox_watch_bus.notify(&id);
   292	
   293	        info!(
   294	            sandbox_id = %id,
   295	            sandbox_name = %name,
   296	            "CreateSandbox request completed successfully"
   297	        );
   298	        Ok(Response::new(SandboxResponse {
   299	            sandbox: Some(sandbox),
   300	        }))
   301	    }

   330	        let state = self.state.clone();

crates/openshell-server/migrations/postgres/003_create_policy_recommendations.sql
-- Draft policy chunks: proposed network policy rules awaiting user approval.
--
-- One row per (sandbox_id, host, port, binary). The toggle model allows:
--   pending -> approved | rejected   (initial decision)
--   approved <-> rejected            (toggle via approve/revoke)
--
-- Upserts bump hit_count / last_seen_ms when the same denial recurs.
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS draft_policy_chunks (
    id              TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    sandbox_id      TEXT NOT NULL,
    draft_version   BIGINT NOT NULL,
    status          TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending',
    rule_name       TEXT NOT NULL,
    proposed_rule   BYTEA NOT NULL,
    rationale       TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
    security_notes  TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
    confidence      DOUBLE PRECISION NOT NULL DEFAULT 0.0,
    host            TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
    port            INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    binary          TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
    hit_count       INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
    first_seen_ms   BIGINT NOT NULL,
    last_seen_ms    BIGINT NOT NULL,
    created_at_ms   BIGINT NOT NULL,
    decided_at_ms   BIGINT
);

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_draft_chunks_sandbox
    ON draft_policy_chunks (sandbox_id, status);

CREATE UNIQUE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_draft_chunks_endpoint
    ON draft_policy_chunks (sandbox_id, host, port, binary)
    WHERE status IN ('pending', 'approved', 'rejected');

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS objects (
    object_type TEXT NOT NULL,
    id TEXT NOT NULL,
    name TEXT NOT NULL,
    payload BYTEA NOT NULL,
    created_at_ms BIGINT NOT NULL,
    updated_at_ms BIGINT NOT NULL,
    PRIMARY KEY (id),
    UNIQUE (object_type, name)
);

CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS sandbox_policies (
    id TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    sandbox_id TEXT NOT NULL,
    version INTEGER NOT NULL,
    policy_payload BYTEA NOT NULL,
    policy_hash TEXT NOT NULL,
    status TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending',
    load_error TEXT,
    created_at_ms BIGINT NOT NULL,
    loaded_at_ms BIGINT,
    UNIQUE (sandbox_id, version)
);

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_sandbox_policies_lookup
    ON sandbox_policies (sandbox_id, version DESC);
crates/openshell-server/migrations/sqlite/003_create_policy_recommendations.sql
-- Draft policy chunks: proposed network policy rules awaiting user approval.
--
-- One row per (sandbox_id, host, port, binary). The toggle model allows:
--   pending -> approved | rejected   (initial decision)
--   approved <-> rejected            (toggle via approve/revoke)
--
-- Upserts bump hit_count / last_seen_ms when the same denial recurs.
CREATE TABLE IF NOT EXISTS draft_policy_chunks (
    id              TEXT PRIMARY KEY,
    sandbox_id      TEXT NOT NULL,
    draft_version   INTEGER NOT NULL,
    status          TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT 'pending',
    rule_name       TEXT NOT NULL,
    proposed_rule   BLOB NOT NULL,
    rationale       TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
    security_notes  TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
    confidence      REAL NOT NULL DEFAULT 0.0,
    host            TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
    port            INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 0,
    binary          TEXT NOT NULL DEFAULT '',
    hit_count       INTEGER NOT NULL DEFAULT 1,
    first_seen_ms   INTEGER NOT NULL,
    last_seen_ms    INTEGER NOT NULL,
    created_at_ms   INTEGER NOT NULL,
    decided_at_ms   INTEGER
);

CREATE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_draft_chunks_sandbox
    ON draft_policy_chunks (sandbox_id, status);

-- Only one active chunk per (sandbox, endpoint, binary). Covers all three
-- statuses so rejected chunks block duplicate proposals until re-approved.
CREATE UNIQUE INDEX IF NOT EXISTS idx_draft_chunks_endpoint
    ON draft_policy_chunks (sandbox_id, host, port, binary)
    WHERE status IN ('pending', 'approved', 'rejected');

   541	    async fn get_sandbox(
   542	        &self,
   543	        request: Request<GetSandboxRequest>,
   544	    ) -> Result<Response<SandboxResponse>, Status> {
   545	        let name = request.into_inner().name;
   546	        if name.is_empty() {
   547	            return Err(Status::invalid_argument("name is required"));
   548	        }
   549	
   550	        let sandbox = self
   551	            .state
   552	            .store
   553	            .get_message_by_name::<Sandbox>(&name)
   554	            .await
   555	            .map_err(|e| Status::internal(format!("fetch sandbox failed: {e}")))?;
   556	
   557	        let sandbox = sandbox.ok_or_else(|| Status::not_found("sandbox not found"))?;
   558	        Ok(Response::new(SandboxResponse {
   559	            sandbox: Some(sandbox),
   560	        }))
   561	    }
   562	
   563	    async fn list_sandboxes(
   564	        &self,
   565	        request: Request<ListSandboxesRequest>,
   566	    ) -> Result<Response<ListSandboxesResponse>, Status> {
   567	        let request = request.into_inner();
   568	        let limit = clamp_limit(request.limit, 100, MAX_PAGE_SIZE);
   569	        let records = self
   570	            .state
   571	            .store
   572	            .list(Sandbox::object_type(), limit, request.offset)
   573	            .await
   574	            .map_err(|e| Status::internal(format!("list sandboxes failed: {e}")))?;
   575	
   576	        let mut sandboxes = Vec::with_capacity(records.len());
   577	        for record in records {
   578	            let mut sandbox = Sandbox::decode(record.payload.as_slice())
   579	                .map_err(|e| Status::internal(format!("decode sandbox failed: {e}")))?;
   580	            sandbox.created_at_ms = record.created_at_ms;
   581	            sandboxes.push(sandbox);
   582	        }
   583	
   584	        Ok(Response::new(ListSandboxesResponse { sandboxes }))
   585	    }

   587	    async fn delete_sandbox(
   588	        &self,
   589	        request: Request<DeleteSandboxRequest>,
   590	    ) -> Result<Response<DeleteSandboxResponse>, Status> {
   591	        let name = request.into_inner().name;

     4	//! `OpenShell` Server library.
     5	//!
     6	//! This crate provides the server implementation for `OpenShell`, including:
     7	//! - gRPC service implementation
     8	//! - HTTP health endpoints
     9	//! - Protocol multiplexing (gRPC + HTTP on same port)
    10	//! - mTLS support
    11

    25

    43	/// Server state shared across handlers.
    44	#[derive(Debug)]
    45	pub struct ServerState {
    46	    /// Server configuration.
    47	    pub config: Config,
    48	
    49	    /// Persistence store.
    50	    pub store: Arc<Store>,
    51	
    52	    /// Kubernetes sandbox client.
    53	    pub sandbox_client: SandboxClient,
    54	
    55	    /// In-memory sandbox correlation index.
    56	    pub sandbox_index: SandboxIndex,
    57	
    58	    /// In-memory bus for sandbox update notifications.
    59	    pub sandbox_watch_bus: SandboxWatchBus,
    60	
    61	    /// In-memory bus for server process logs.
    62	    pub tracing_log_bus: TracingLogBus,
    63	
    64	    /// Active SSH tunnel connection counts per session token.
    65	    pub ssh_connections_by_token: Mutex<HashMap<String, u32>>,
    66	
    67	    /// Active SSH tunnel connection counts per sandbox id.
    68	    pub ssh_connections_by_sandbox: Mutex<HashMap<String, u32>>,
    69	
    70	    /// Serializes settings mutations (global and sandbox) to prevent
    71	    /// read-modify-write races. Held for the duration of any setting
    72	    /// set/delete operation, including the precedence check on sandbox
    73	    /// mutations that reads global state.
    74	    pub settings_mutex: tokio::sync::Mutex<()>,
    75	}
    76	
    77	fn is_benign_tls_handshake_failure(error: &std::io::Error) -> bool {
    78	    matches!(
    79	        error.kind(),
    80	        ErrorKind::UnexpectedEof | ErrorKind::ConnectionReset
    81	    )
    82	}
    83	
    84	impl ServerState {
    85	    /// Create new server state.
    86	    #[must_use]
    87	    pub fn new(
    88	        config: Config,
    89	        store: Arc<Store>,
    90	        sandbox_client: SandboxClient,
    91	        sandbox_index: SandboxIndex,
    92	        sandbox_watch_bus: SandboxWatchBus,
    93	        tracing_log_bus: TracingLogBus,
    94	    ) -> Self {
    95	        Self {
    96	            config,
    97	            store,
    98	            sandbox_client,
    99	            sandbox_index,
   100	            sandbox_watch_bus,
   101	            tracing_log_bus,
   102	            ssh_connections_by_token: Mutex::new(HashMap::new()),
   103	            ssh_connections_by_sandbox: Mutex::new(HashMap::new()),
   104	            settings_mutex: tokio::sync::Mutex::new(()),
   105	        }
   106	    }
   107	}
   108	
   109	/// Run the `OpenShell` server.
   110	///
   111	/// This starts a multiplexed gRPC/HTTP server on the configured bind address.
   112	///
   113	/// # Errors
   114	///
   115	/// Returns an error if the server fails to start or encounters a fatal error.
   116	pub async fn run_server(config: Config, tracing_log_bus: TracingLogBus) -> Result<()> {
   117	    let database_url = config.database_url.trim();
   118	    if database_url.is_empty() {
   119	        return Err(Error::config("database_url is required"));
   120	    }
   121	    if config.ssh_handshake_secret.is_empty() {
   122	        return Err(Error::config(
   123	            "ssh_handshake_secret is required. Set --ssh-handshake-secret or OPENSHELL_SSH_HANDSHAKE_SECRET",
   124	        ));
   125	    }
   126	
   127	    let store = Store::connect(database_url).await?;
   128	    let sandbox_client = SandboxClient::new(
   129	        config.sandbox_namespace.clone(),
   130	        config.sandbox_image.clone(),
   131	        config.sandbox_image_pull_policy.clone(),
   132	        config.grpc_endpoint.clone(),
   133	        format!("0.0.0.0:{}", config.sandbox_ssh_port),
   134	        config.ssh_handshake_secret.clone(),
   135	        config.ssh_handshake_skew_secs,
   136	        config.client_tls_secret_name.clone(),
   137	        config.host_gateway_ip.clone(),
   138	    )
   139	    .await
   140	    .map_err(|e| Error::execution(format!("failed to create kubernetes client: {e}")))?;
   141	    let store = Arc::new(store);
   142	
   143	    let sandbox_index = SandboxIndex::new();
   144	    let sandbox_watch_bus = SandboxWatchBus::new();
   145	    let state = Arc::new(ServerState::new(
   146	        config.clone(),
   147	        store.clone(),
   148	        sandbox_client,
   149	        sandbox_index,
   150	        sandbox_watch_bus,
   151	        tracing_log_bus,
   152	    ));
   153	
   154	    spawn_sandbox_watcher(
   155	        store.clone(),
   156	        state.sandbox_client.clone(),
   157	        state.sandbox_index.clone(),
   158	        state.sandbox_watch_bus.clone(),
   159	        state.tracing_log_bus.clone(),
   160	    );
   161	    spawn_store_reconciler(
   162	        store.clone(),
   163	        state.sandbox_client.clone(),
   164	        state.sandbox_index.clone(),
   165	        state.sandbox_watch_bus.clone(),
   166	        state.tracing_log_bus.clone(),
   167	    );
   168	    spawn_kube_event_tailer(state.clone());
   169	    ssh_tunnel::spawn_session_reaper(store.clone(), std::time::Duration::from_secs(3600));
   170	
   171	    // Create the multiplexed service
   172	    let service = MultiplexService::new(state.clone());
   173	
   174	    // Bind the TCP listener
   175	    let listener = TcpListener::bind(config.bind_address)
   176	        .await
   177	        .map_err(|e| Error::transport(format!("failed to bind to {}: {e}", config.bind_address)))?;
   178	
   179	    info!(address = %config.bind_address, "Server listening");
   180

    64	        Ok(SandboxPhase::Deleting) => "Deleting",
    65	        Ok(SandboxPhase::Unknown) | Err(_) => "Unknown",
    66	    }

  1841	#[allow(clippy::too_many_arguments)]
  1842	pub async fn sandbox_create_with_bootstrap(
  1843	    name: Option<&str>,
  1844	    from: Option<&str>,
  1845	    upload: Option<&(String, Option<String>, bool)>,

  1862	             Set one with: openshell gateway select <name>\n\

  1868	        crate::bootstrap::run_bootstrap(remote, ssh_key, requested_gpu).await?;

  1870	    // failure right after deploy does not trigger a second bootstrap attempt.

  1895	    keep: bool,
  1896	    forward: Option<&openshell_core::forward::ForwardSpec>,
  1897	) -> bool {

  1901	async fn finalize_sandbox_create_session(
  1902	    server: &str,
  1903	    sandbox_name: &str,
  1904	    persist: bool,
  1905	    session_result: Result<()>,
  1906	    tls: &TlsOptions,
  1907	    gateway: &str,
  1908	) -> Result<()> {
  1909	    if persist {
  1910	        return session_result;
  1911	    }
  1912

  1916	            return Err(err);
  1917	        }
  1918	        eprintln!("Failed to delete sandbox {sandbox_name}: {err}");
  1919	    }
  1920	
  1921	    session_result
  1922	}

  1924	/// Create a sandbox with default settings.
  1925	#[allow(clippy::too_many_arguments)]
  1926	pub async fn sandbox_create(
  1927	    server: &str,
  1928	    name: Option<&str>,
  1929	    from: Option<&str>,
  1930	    gateway_name: &str,
  1931	    upload: Option<&(String, Option<String>, bool)>,
  1932	    keep: bool,
  1933	    gpu: bool,
  1934	    editor: Option<Editor>,
  1935	    remote: Option<&str>,
  1936	    ssh_key: Option<&str>,
  1937	    providers: &[String],
  1938	    policy: Option<&str>,
  1939	    forward: Option<openshell_core::forward::ForwardSpec>,
  1940	    command: &[String],
  1941	    tty_override: Option<bool>,
  1942	    bootstrap_override: Option<bool>,
  1943	    auto_providers_override: Option<bool>,
  1944	    tls: &TlsOptions,
  1945	) -> Result<()> {
  1946	    if editor.is_some() && !command.is_empty() {
  1947	        return Err(miette::miette!(
  1948	            "--editor cannot be used with a trailing command; use `openshell sandbox connect <name> --editor ...` after the sandbox is ready"
  1949	        ));
  1950	    }
  1951	
  1952	    // Check port availability *before* creating the sandbox so we don't
  1953	    // leave an orphaned sandbox behind when the forward would fail.
  1954	    if let Some(ref spec) = forward {
  1955	        openshell_core::forward::check_port_available(spec)?;
  1956	    }
  1957	
  1958	    // Try connecting to the gateway. If the connection fails due to a
  1959	    // connectivity error and bootstrap is allowed, start a new gateway.
  1960	    //
  1961	    // bootstrap_override is Some(false) when:
  1962	    //   - the user passed --no-bootstrap
  1963	    //   - an existing gateway was already resolved (don't replace it)
  1964	    //   - we already bootstrapped once (don't double-bootstrap)
  1965	    let (mut client, effective_server, effective_tls) = match grpc_client(server, tls).await {
  1966	        Ok(c) => (c, server.to_string(), tls.clone()),
  1967	        Err(err) => {
  1968	            if !crate::bootstrap::should_attempt_bootstrap(&err, tls) {
  1969	                return Err(err);
  1970	            }
  1971	            if !crate::bootstrap::confirm_bootstrap(bootstrap_override)? {
  1972	                // The gateway is configured but not reachable. Give the user
  1973	                // actionable recovery steps instead of a raw connection error.
  1974	                eprintln!();
  1975	                eprintln!(
  1976	                    "{} Gateway '{}' is not reachable.",
  1977	                    "!".yellow(),
  1978	                    gateway_name,
  1979	                );
  1980	                eprintln!();
  1981	                eprintln!("  To destroy and recreate the gateway:");
  1982	                eprintln!();
  1983	                eprintln!(
  1984	                    "    {} && {}",
  1985	                    format!("openshell gateway destroy --name {gateway_name}").cyan(),
  1986	                    "openshell gateway start".cyan(),
  1987	                );
  1988	                eprintln!();
  1989	                return Err(err);
  1990	            }
  1991	            let requested_gpu = gpu || from.is_some_and(source_requests_gpu);
  1992	            let (new_tls, new_server, _) =
  1993	                crate::bootstrap::run_bootstrap(remote, ssh_key, requested_gpu).await?;
  1994	            let c = grpc_client(&new_server, &new_tls)
  1995	                .await
  1996	                .wrap_err("bootstrap succeeded but failed to connect to gateway")?;
  1997	            (c, new_server, new_tls)
  1998	        }
  1999	    };
  2000	
  2001	    // Resolve the --from flag into a container image reference, building from
  2002	    // a Dockerfile first if necessary.
  2003	    let image: Option<String> = match from {
  2004	        Some(val) => {
  2005	            let resolved = resolve_from(val)?;
  2006	            match resolved {
  2007	                ResolvedSource::Image(img) => Some(img),
  2008	                ResolvedSource::Dockerfile {
  2009	                    dockerfile,
  2010	                    context,
  2011	                } => {
  2012	                    let tag = build_from_dockerfile(&dockerfile, &context, gateway_name).await?;
  2013	                    Some(tag)
  2014	                }
  2015	            }
  2016	        }
  2017	        None => None,
  2018	    };
  2019	    let requested_gpu = gpu || image.as_deref().is_some_and(image_requests_gpu);
  2020	
  2021	    let inferred_types: Vec<String> = inferred_provider_type(command).into_iter().collect();
  2022	    let configured_providers = ensure_required_providers(
  2023	        &mut client,
  2024	        providers,
  2025	        &inferred_types,
  2026	        auto_providers_override,
  2027	    )
  2028	    .await?;
  2029	
  2030	    let policy = load_sandbox_policy(policy)?;
  2031	
  2032	    let template = image.map(|img| SandboxTemplate {

  2034	        ..SandboxTemplate::default()
  2035	    });
  2036	
  2037	    let request = CreateSandboxRequest {
  2038	        spec: Some(SandboxSpec {
  2039	            gpu: requested_gpu,
  2040	            policy,
  2041	            providers: configured_providers,
  2042	            template,

    15	    load_gateway_metadata, load_last_sandbox, save_last_sandbox,
    16	};
    17	use openshell_cli::completers;
    18	use openshell_cli::run;
    19	use openshell_cli::tls::TlsOptions;
    20	
    21	/// Resolved gateway context: name + gateway endpoint.
    22	struct GatewayContext {
    23	    /// The gateway name (used for TLS cert directory, metadata lookup, etc.).
    24	    name: String,
    25	    /// The gateway endpoint URL (e.g., `https://127.0.0.1` or `https://10.0.0.5`).
    26	    endpoint: String,
    27	}
    28	
    29	/// Resolve the gateway name to a [`GatewayContext`] with the gateway endpoint.
    30	///
    31	/// Resolution priority:
    32	/// 1. `--gateway-endpoint` flag (direct URL, preserving metadata when available)
    33	/// 2. `--gateway` flag (explicit name)
    34	/// 3. `OPENSHELL_GATEWAY` environment variable
    35	/// 4. Active gateway from `~/.config/openshell/active_gateway`
    36	///
    37	/// When `--gateway-endpoint` is provided, it is used directly as the endpoint.
    38	/// If stored metadata can still identify the gateway, the stored gateway name
    39	/// is preserved so auth and TLS materials continue to resolve correctly.
    40	fn normalize_gateway_endpoint(endpoint: &str) -> &str {
    41	    endpoint.trim_end_matches('/')
    42	}
    43	
    44	fn find_gateway_by_endpoint(endpoint: &str) -> Option<String> {
    45	    let endpoint = normalize_gateway_endpoint(endpoint);
    46	
    47	    if let Some(active_name) = load_active_gateway()
    48	        && let Ok(metadata) = load_gateway_metadata(&active_name)
    49	        && normalize_gateway_endpoint(&metadata.gateway_endpoint) == endpoint
    50	    {
    51	        return Some(metadata.name);
    52	    }
    53	
    54	    list_gateways().ok()?.into_iter().find_map(|metadata| {
    55	        (normalize_gateway_endpoint(&metadata.gateway_endpoint) == endpoint)
    56	            .then_some(metadata.name)
    57	    })
    58	}
    59	
    60	fn resolve_gateway(
    61	    gateway_flag: &Option<String>,
    62	    gateway_endpoint: &Option<String>,
    63	) -> Result<GatewayContext> {
    64	    if let Some(endpoint) = gateway_endpoint {
    65	        let name = gateway_flag
    66	            .clone()
    67	            .filter(|name| get_gateway_metadata(name).is_some())
    68	            .or_else(|| find_gateway_by_endpoint(endpoint))
    69	            .unwrap_or_else(|| endpoint.clone());
    70	        return Ok(GatewayContext {
    71	            name,
    72	            endpoint: endpoint.clone(),
    73	        });
    74	    }
    75	
    76	    let name = gateway_flag
    77	        .clone()
    78	        .or_else(|| {
    79	            std::env::var("OPENSHELL_GATEWAY")
    80	                .ok()

   188	#[tokio::test]
   189	async fn sqlite_name_unique_per_object_type() {
   190	    let store = Store::connect("sqlite::memory:?cache=shared")
   191	        .await
   192	        .unwrap();
   193	
   194	    store
   195	        .put("sandbox", "id-1", "shared-name", b"payload1")
   196	        .await
   197	        .unwrap();
   198	
   199	    // Same name, same object_type, different id -> should fail (unique constraint).
   200	    let result = store
   201	        .put("sandbox", "id-2", "shared-name", b"payload2")
   202	        .await;
   203	    assert!(result.is_err());
   204	
   205	    // Same name, different object_type -> should succeed.
   206	    store
   207	        .put("secret", "id-3", "shared-name", b"payload3")
   208	        .await
   209	        .unwrap();
   210	}

   212	#[tokio::test]
   213	async fn sqlite_id_globally_unique() {
   214	    let store = Store::connect("sqlite::memory:?cache=shared")
   215	        .await
   216	        .unwrap();
   217	
   218	    store
   219	        .put("sandbox", "same-id", "name-a", b"payload1")
   220	        .await
   221	        .unwrap();
   222	
   223	    // Same id, different object_type -> the upsert is a no-op (WHERE
   224	    // clause prevents updating a row with a different object_type).
   225	    // The original row is preserved unchanged.
   226	    store
   227	        .put("secret", "same-id", "name-b", b"payload2")
   228	        .await
   229	        .unwrap();
   230	
   231	    // Original row is untouched.
   232	    let record = store.get("sandbox", "same-id").await.unwrap().unwrap();
   233	    assert_eq!(record.object_type, "sandbox");
   234	    assert_eq!(record.payload, b"payload1");
   235	
   236	    // The secret was not inserted.
   237	    let missing = store.get("secret", "same-id").await.unwrap();
   238	    assert!(missing.is_none());
   239	}

  4041	/// Redact credential values from a provider before returning it in a gRPC
  4042	/// response.  Key names are preserved so callers can display credential counts
  4043	/// and key listings.  Internal server paths (inference routing, sandbox env
  4044	/// injection) read credentials from the store directly and are unaffected.
  4045	fn redact_provider_credentials(mut provider: Provider) -> Provider {
  4046	    for value in provider.credentials.values_mut() {
  4047	        *value = "REDACTED".to_string();
  4048	    }
  4049	    provider

/// Validate field sizes on a `CreateSandboxRequest` before persisting.
///
/// Returns `INVALID_ARGUMENT` on the first field that exceeds its limit.
fn validate_sandbox_spec(
    name: &str,
    spec: &openshell_core::proto::SandboxSpec,
) -> Result<(), Status> {
    // --- request.name ---
    if name.len() > MAX_NAME_LEN {
        return Err(Status::invalid_argument(format!(
            "name exceeds maximum length ({} > {MAX_NAME_LEN})",
            name.len()
        )));
    }

    // --- spec.providers ---
    if spec.providers.len() > MAX_PROVIDERS {
        return Err(Status::invalid_argument(format!(
            "providers list exceeds maximum ({} > {MAX_PROVIDERS})",
            spec.providers.len()
        )));
    }

    // --- spec.log_level ---
    if spec.log_level.len() > MAX_LOG_LEVEL_LEN {
        return Err(Status::invalid_argument(format!(
            "log_level exceeds maximum length ({} > {MAX_LOG_LEVEL_LEN})",
            spec.log_level.len()
        )));
    }

    // --- spec.environment ---
    validate_string_map(
        &spec.environment,
        MAX_ENVIRONMENT_ENTRIES,
        MAX_MAP_KEY_LEN,
        MAX_MAP_VALUE_LEN,
        "spec.environment",
    )?;

    // --- spec.template ---
    if let Some(ref tmpl) = spec.template {
        validate_sandbox_template(tmpl)?;
    }

    // --- spec.policy serialized size ---
    if let Some(ref policy) = spec.policy {
        let size = policy.encoded_len();
        if size > MAX_POLICY_SIZE {
            return Err(Status::invalid_argument(format!(
                "policy serialized size exceeds maximum ({size} > {MAX_POLICY_SIZE})"
            )));
        }
    }

    Ok(())
}

/// Validate template-level field sizes.
fn validate_sandbox_template(tmpl: &SandboxTemplate) -> Result<(), Status> {
    // String fields.
    for (field, value) in [
        ("template.image", &tmpl.image),
        ("template.runtime_class_name", &tmpl.runtime_class_name),
        ("template.agent_socket", &tmpl.agent_socket),
    ] {
        if value.len() > MAX_TEMPLATE_STRING_LEN {
            return Err(Status::invalid_argument(format!(
                "{field} exceeds maximum length ({} > {MAX_TEMPLATE_STRING_LEN})",
                value.len()
            )));
        }
    }

    // Map fields.
    validate_string_map(
        &tmpl.labels,
        MAX_TEMPLATE_MAP_ENTRIES,
        MAX_MAP_KEY_LEN,
        MAX_MAP_VALUE_LEN,
        "template.labels",
    )?;
    validate_string_map(
        &tmpl.annotations,
        MAX_TEMPLATE_MAP_ENTRIES,

     4	//! In-memory indexes for correlating Kubernetes objects back to sandbox ids.
     5	
     6	use std::collections::HashMap;
     7	use std::sync::{Arc, RwLock};
     8	
     9	use openshell_core::proto::Sandbox;
    10	
    11	#[derive(Debug, Clone, Default)]
    12	pub struct SandboxIndex {
    13	    inner: Arc<RwLock<Inner>>,
    14	}
    15	
    16	#[derive(Debug, Default)]
    17	struct Inner {
    18	    sandbox_name_to_id: HashMap<String, String>,
    19	    agent_pod_to_id: HashMap<String, String>,
    20	}
    21	
    22	impl SandboxIndex {
    23	    #[must_use]
    24	    pub fn new() -> Self {
    25	        Self::default()
    26	    }
    27	
    28	    pub fn update_from_sandbox(&self, sandbox: &Sandbox) {
    29	        let mut inner = self.inner.write().expect("sandbox index lock poisoned");
    30	        if !sandbox.name.is_empty() {
    31	            inner
    32	                .sandbox_name_to_id
    33	                .insert(sandbox.name.clone(), sandbox.id.clone());
    34	        }
    35	
    36	        if let Some(status) = sandbox.status.as_ref()
    37	            && !status.agent_pod.is_empty()
    38	        {
    39	            inner
    40	                .agent_pod_to_id
    41	                .insert(status.agent_pod.clone(), sandbox.id.clone());
    42	        }
    43	    }
    44	
    45	    pub fn remove_sandbox(&self, sandbox_id: &str) {
    46	        let mut inner = self.inner.write().expect("sandbox index lock poisoned");
    47	        inner.sandbox_name_to_id.retain(|_, v| v != sandbox_id);
    48	        inner.agent_pod_to_id.retain(|_, v| v != sandbox_id);
    49	    }
    50	
    51	    #[must_use]
    52	    pub fn sandbox_id_for_sandbox_name(&self, name: &str) -> Option<String> {
    53	        let inner = self.inner.read().expect("sandbox index lock poisoned");
    54	        inner.sandbox_name_to_id.get(name).cloned()
    55	    }
    56	
    57	    #[must_use]

    60	        inner.agent_pod_to_id.get(pod).cloned()
    61	    }

+fn format_create_sandbox_status(status: Status) -> miette::Report {
+    if status.code() == Code::AlreadyExists {
+        return miette::miette!(status.message().to_string());
+    }
+
+    miette::miette!("{status}")
+}

+fn sandbox_already_exists_status(name: &str) -> Status {
+    Status::already_exists(format!(
+        "sandbox '{name}' already exists\n\n\
+         hint: delete it first with: openshell sandbox delete {name}\n\
+               or use a different name"
+    ))
+}
+
+fn is_unique_name_constraint_error(message: &str) -> bool {
+    message.contains("objects.object_type, objects.name")
+        || message.contains("objects_object_type_name_key")
+        || message.contains("UNIQUE constraint failed: objects.object_type, objects.name")
+}
